SELECT partNumber, modelName, price * 0.5 AS reducedPrice, brand FROM parts WHERE LOWER(brand) = 'bmw' ORDER BY reducedPrice DESC;
Get all bmw parts and reduce their price by 50%

**********************************************************************************************
SELECT partNumber, modelName, price * 0.85 AS reducedPrice, brand, year FROM parts WHERE LOWER(brand) = 'polaris' AND year > 2018 ORDER BY price DESC;
Get all parts from polaris that were made after 2018 and reduce their price by 15%
There are no parts from the brand Polaris that were manufactured after 2018 in the database.
**********************************************************************************************
SELECT partNumber, modelName, price * 0.85 AS reducedPrice, brand, year FROM parts WHERE LOWER(brand) IN ('polaris', 'indian') AND year > 2018 ORDER BY price DESC;
Get all parts from polaris/indian that were made after 2018 and reduce their price by 15%
There are no parts from the brands Polaris or Indian that were released after 2018 in the database.
**********************************************************************************************
SELECT partNumber, modelName, price * 0.5 AS reduced_price, brand, year, description FROM parts WHERE LOWER(description) LIKE '%used%'
Get all used parts and reduce their price by 50%

SELECT partNumber, modelName, price * 0.6 AS reducedPrice, quantity FROM parts WHERE quantity > 2 ORDER BY price DESC;
Get all parts that have more than 2 on quantity and reduce their price by 40%
